< text>
Unfortunately I wish I had something better to say about this local business. I have rented before from another company in Hesperia and when I moved  to Victorville decided to try this company because of its location nearby. This was a mistake. I reserved the storage unit online because the website said there was ‚Äúno obligation‚Äù and that I could come in and finalize the signatures and contract. The website also said that the first month was no cost just a $29.00 move in rate.

So the same day (Friday) I went in and spoke with the manager who was nice. As we were reviewing the contract she stated the cost due and I advise about the online pricing. She took a moment to review the information and then confirmed that I was right and the monthly price of $149 would be due the following month in March. We proceeded to sign the contact.

I then came in 3 days later  on Monday (I would have come earlier but they are closed on Sundays) and advised that my father in law did not need the unit anymore and we would need to cancel. I first offered to move to a smaller unit but none were available. I said even though we did not move anything in I understand that we have to pay the $29. But the manager stated we would be charge the first month fee of $149. I reminded her about the conversation we had before I signed and she stated that she made a mistake when she told me I would not be charged until March. Unfortunately she is the manager and I will have to wait 6 days to find out if I would be issued some sort of refund and 6-8 weeks to receive anything in the mail.

She admitted it was her error and yet I will be the one that has to pay the price for her mistake. No accountability. Poor customer service.

There are plenty of other storage units in the HD that would like mine and your business.< /text>

***UPDATE JUNE 2020***
(STAR RATE INCREASE from 2-Star TO 5-Star)

Upon reaching out to Management with Stor-America, we came to a reasonable rate. I am EXTREMELY APPRECIATIVE for them extending this courtesy to me.  The interactions with staff and Kimberly, the Mgr. have been consistently professional and kind.

THANK YOU STOR AMERICA for providing a long-termer like myself a decent and safe storage.

This facility has undergone many changes and endured some hardships along the way.  Over the course of my ongoing tenancy here, they seem to be coming onto the upswing of their business. So glad they have found some success through these very challenging times.  WORTH SUPPORTING LOCAL businesses, like this one.

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++

(PREVIOUS REVIEW BELOW)

Moved into this nice storage facility in March 2014. The staff was very accommodating and professional.  Juan, Ashley and another gal whose name I sadly cannot recall all were so helpful in the account setup and move in process. The introductory move in special made it possible to choose this location hands down for affordability and convenience of location.

LOVED that they offer a Free truck for moving in, it really made the whole matter very stress-free! THANK YOU for making me feel very welcome!

Fast-forward 5 yrs, Mgt. has changed a few times and increases have happened annually.  I can understand to a point why this happens, however as of July 2019 the rate increased from $87 to $102 for a 5x10. (And that is without the additional insurance, which I had to cancel due to inability to afford the extra $10 monthly fee)

I wish to remain a loyal and devoted customer, tho it has vastly become a burden to meet these rates. Can only pray they could work with me on keeping my storage affordable.< /review>

This is the best fish market in Long Beach! I want to give 5 stars, however, I believe customer service experience plays a part in ratings so I cannot give a 5. When ordering my food over the phone and coming to pick it up I feel rushed and as if the person on the other end is snappy and rude. This has happened on 3 separate occasions. It's a big job to keep a store filled with so many diverse items neat and presentable.  The ladies who work here are very friendly and welcome you when you go in. There's a quirky guy who works in furniture who may seem grumpy at times but in general he is very helpful if you just ask.
I find so many deals that are much better than big box stores and get my daughters art canvasses here and some school supplies throughout the year when other stores are out or simply too expensive.
If you live in Lomita or in South Torrance shop where you live to keep the stores we enjoy open.< /review>
